posted:Posted November 28, 2023
msg:Crowne Plaza Guangzhou Huadu: Single Travel Diary

Now that InterContinental's advanced rewards reach 100 nights per year, there are no new follow-ups. This is quite a dampener for business travelers like us who stay out for more than 100 nights every year. Of the 11 districts in Guangzhou, Conghua and Nansha currently do not have InterContinental hotels. Most of the other districts have one InterContinental hotel in each district, with the exception of Huadu District (two: R&F Airport Holidays and Huadu CP). Turn left 50 meters out of the Huadu CP lobby and you will find Exit D of Qingtang Metro Station. It takes exactly one hour to get to Xingang East Station (Pazhou Convention and Exhibition Center). For me, it is very convenient (the most important thing is no traffic jam). The hotel has a Huadu gourmet area for breakfast, freshly squeezed juice and a children's area. The gym has complete equipment, as well as niche equipment such as fascia guns, which is very attentive. The swimming pool is outdoors, and you can reach it through the small garden (the garden design rules of the entire hotel highlight the agility, I like this style very much).‚Äã‚Äã

In the past, HIX hotels around the airport have been delisted. Currently, among the intercontinental hotels, there are three that are close to the airport: R&F Airport Holidays, Nanhu Holidays, and Huadu CP. Like R&F Airport HI, Huadu CP has a shuttle bus, which is very convenient to the airport. Of course, the driver is not as enthusiastic as R&F Airport Holidays and never knows how to help guests with their luggage. On the other hand, the bellboy and concierge manager of Huadu CP are very attentive and attentive, which must be praised. There are many opportunities to meet flight attendants in Huadu CP, such as outside the hotel lobby, at the front desk, etc. You will often see flight attendants from famous airlines such as Singapore Airlines and China Southern Airlines, similar to Ho Chi Minh Intercontinental, on super buses, on There are Asiana Airlines stewardesses all over the place. I‚Äôm not writing this to explain anything, I just want to emphasize that Huadu CP is an airport-type hotel, which is very suitable for business trip parties, that‚Äôs all, haha. Because the buildings around the airport have limited high-rise requirements, this hotel is destined not to be a high-floor hotel. This is due to the special location and is definitely not because the Chinese owner is weak.‚Äã‚Äã

In the past, they were given upgraded suites, executive trea**ent, and 90 yuan meal coupons. This time, except for simple welcome fruits and routine welcome drink coupons, there was nothing. In prosperous years, hotels with good business, and large top-end high-end hotels will hold a grand lighting ceremony a month before Chris**as Eve (that is, from this day on, the Chris**as tree will be lit up and will continue until the New Year. When heavyweight guests or senior executives come to light the lights, they actually press the switch, which is mainly a blessing ceremony.) More than ten years ago, I hosted the Wangfujing Pedestrian Street lighting ceremony, Lane Crawford lighting ceremony, and the Westin Financial Street lighting ceremony in Beijing. Lighting Ceremony, Shangri-La Lighting Ceremony, Kerry Center Lighting Ceremony, etc. In lean years, hotels with flat business and non-peak hotels will quietly put up a Chris**as tree as a decoration for the entire month before Chris**as Eve (of course, it will not be as eye-catching as the one at the Waldorf Astoria in Beijing) , other details will also be simply decorated, such as Chris**as hats on the revolving doors of this Huadu CP, and small-scale decorations on the entrance to the gym.‚Äã‚Äã

Many people think that being a professional car host means staying in a hotel every day and being happy. In fact, this is a huge misunderstanding. The auto show host industry is extremely low-level and extremely hard. I always have the most words. This is a well-known thing. I have performed five performances a day, each of 20 minutes, in a noisy exhibition hall for seventeen years. , this is physical work, and it is also hard work. It is like exchanging M for Q. Everyone only saw Z eating meat, but not Z being beaten. Some booths cannot compete with you, so they can only rely on voice suppression or various complaints to trap you. The happiest and most liberating moments every day almost always come from the process of escaping from the exhibition hall and staying in a hotel after get off work. This is a kind of cultural baptism and the best way to release long-term depression. For example, one time I stayed at CP in Huadu, and it happened to be New Year‚Äôs Eve. The hotel found that I was alone on a business trip, and specially gave me a coupon for the dinner buffet to let me relax. This kind of warm and gentle small blessing may not be common to ordinary people. People who are on business trips and don‚Äôt always stay in hotels can‚Äôt understand it.
